***reedy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reedy.html>reedy</a> (67832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:reedy.html>reedy</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">reedi</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">reeddy</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:reed.html>reed</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:reedy.html>reedy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">reedier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">reediest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Full of, or edged with, <a href = vnd.unilang:reeds.html>reeds</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a sound or voice</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> High and thin in tone.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a person</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Tall and thin.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metallurgy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Imperfectly welded together in masses of rods.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:reedy.html>reedy</a></b> iron</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***reefer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reefer.html>reefer</a> (67831)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">reef</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:reefer.html>reefer</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">reefers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who reefs sails, especially a midshipman.
<ul><li><b>1922</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Katherine_Mansfield" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Katherine Mansfield">Katherine Mansfield</a>, ‘Prelude’, Oxford 2002 (<i>Selected <a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>Stories</a></i>), p. 85:
<dl><dd>Her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:reefer.html>reefer</a></b> cap <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> all on one side and on her cheek there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the print of an anchor button she <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> pressed on while sleeping.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1905</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Masefield" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Masefield">John Masefield</a>, <i>Sea Life in Nelson's Times</i>, p. 27:
<dl><dd>The mess table, at which the <b>reefers</b> and mates made merry, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> fixed in the middle of the berth.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:reefer.html>reefer</a> jacket; a close-fitting jacket or short coat of thick cloth.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:reefer.html>reefer</a> jacket</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Clipping of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">refrigerator</i></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:reefer.html>reefer</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">reefers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A refrigerated, insulated trailer, ship or shipping container.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1988</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jane.html>Jane</a> Stern amp; ‎Michael Stern,  <cite>A taste of America</cite>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 41:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Next to the cash register, a bulletin board <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> thumbtacked with notes from deadheaders who needed loads heading west, and shippers <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> for a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:reefer.html>reefer</a></b> (refrigerated <a href = vnd.unilang:truck.html>truck</a>) going down to Florida.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rail transport<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/refrigerator_car" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:refrigerator car">refrigerator car</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">type of <a href = vnd.unilang:boxcar.html>boxcar</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Origin uncertain. Perhaps from regional <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">grifa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cannabis</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Mexico), <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">grifo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:smokes.html>smokes</a> cannabis</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Central America).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:reefer.html>reefer</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">reefers</b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A marijuana cigarette.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Marijuana.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1982</b>,  Edward G. <a href = vnd.unilang:fletcher.html>Fletcher</a>; Melle <a href = vnd.unilang:mel.html>Mel</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>lyrics</a> and music),  “The Message”, in  <cite>The Message</cite>, performed by <a href = vnd.unilang:grandmaster.html>Grandmaster</a> Flash:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Daddy I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> want to go to school because the teacher's a jerk, he must think I'm a fool and all the kids smoke <b><a href = vnd.unilang:reefer.html>reefer</a></b>, I think it'd be cheaper if I just got a job learned to be a street sweeper.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">marijuana cigarette</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> See also Thesaurus:marijuana cigarette, Appendix:Cannabis <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></li></ul>
</body>

***reeks.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reeks.html>reeks</a> (6380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">raecs</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">reecs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rakis</i>, of uncertain origin.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reeks.html>reeks</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reeksen.html>reeksen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reeks.html>reeksje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A series, a sequence.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verspil.html>Verspil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lezen.html>lezen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betekenisloos.html>betekenisloze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:reeks.html>reeks</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do not waste your time on reading that meaningless <b>sequence</b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rij.html>rij</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:serie.html>serie</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A series of print publications.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enorm.html>enorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boze.html>boze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brieven.html>brieven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgever.html>uitgever</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sturen.html>sturen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eis.html>eis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:reeks.html>reeks</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:stopzetten.html>stopzetten</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I am going to write an enormous quantity of angry <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a> to the publisher with the demand that they will cancel the <b>series</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***reep.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reep.html>reep</a> (12277)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rep</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:reep.html>reep</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">reip</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">rēp</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raipaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rope, cord, <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a>, ringlet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*roypnós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strap, <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a>, rope</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:reep.html>Reep</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Reif</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">reap</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rope</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">reipi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rope</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reep.html>reep</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:repen.html>repen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reepje.html>reepje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a <span class="Latn" lang="en">strip</span>, resulting from ripping, cutting etc.</li>
<li>a <span class="Latn" lang="en">rope</span></li>
<li>a <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a></li>
<li>an edible <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a></span>, esp. a <span class="Latn" lang="en">candy <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a></span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:rijten.html>rete</a></i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:referentie.html>referentie</a> (15499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Presumably in each sense independently derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">référence</i>, presumably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">referer</i> (14th century), anyway from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">referre</i> "to relate, refer", literally "to carry back", itself from re- "back" + ferre "to carry, bring"
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:referentie.html>referentie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:referenties.html>referenties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:referentie.html>referentietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A reference, person who vouches for another, character witness</li>
<li>A quoted or otherwise consulted, preferably reliably or authoritative source, as for writing an academic document</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bankreferentie</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">handelsreferentie</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:referentiekader.html>referentiekader</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">referentiemonster</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">referentiepunt</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***referentiekader.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:referentiekader.html>referentiekader</a> (88863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:referentie.html>referentie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reference</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kader.html>kader</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">frame</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:referentiekader.html>referentiekader</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:referentiekaders.html>referentiekaders</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:referentiekader.html>referentiekadertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>frame of reference
<ol><li>system of organising thought containing prior beliefs</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> diagram or system from where an observer observes (relative) motion</li></ol></li></ol>

***reflectie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reflectie.html>reflectie</a> (17458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">reflexion</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">reflection</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">reflexio</i>, from the participle <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:reflecteren.html>reflectere</a></i>. The current spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">reflect</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reflectie.html>reflectie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reflecties.html>reflecties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reflectie.html>reflectietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">reflection</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">thought</span> about something</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">terugkaatsing</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weerkaatsing.html>weerkaatsing</a></span></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">reformēren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">reformer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">reformer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">refōrmō</i>.

***regel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:regel.html>regel</a> (976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:regel.html>regel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rēgula</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regel.html>regel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regels.html>regels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regelen.html>regelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regel.html>regeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>line of writing, verse; (pre-printed) straight line to write it on</li>
<li>rule, regulation, custom, prescript</li>
<li>narrow slat; especially a ruler</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:regenachtig.html>regenachtig</a> (56168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regen.html>regen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-achtig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-like, -ish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li>rainy, prone to rain

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">regendrup</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">regendrop</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*regandropo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*regnadrupô</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regen.html>regen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:druppel.html>druppel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drop, droplet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***regenen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:regenen.html>regenen</a> (5614)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rēgenen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*reganon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*regnōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regen.html>regen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:regenen.html>regenen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To rain, to precipitate.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:regent.html>regent</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:alweer.html>alweer</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>It's <b>raining</b> again.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To accumulate in large amounts, as though by rain
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:regent.html>regent</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:klachten.html>klachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedrag.html>gedrag</a>!</i>
<dl><dd>It's <b>raining</b> complaints about your behaviour!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To pour down, to fall out of the sky in large amounts
<dl><dd><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:herfst.html>herfst</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:regenen.html>regenen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bladeren.html>bladeren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bomen.html>bomen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>In autumn, the leaves <b>rain</b> down from the trees.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:regenwater.html>regenwater</a></i>. ***registratie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:registratie.html>registratie</a> (13537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From obsolete (middle?) French registration (modern cognate enrégistrement) or directly from Middle <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">registratio</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">registrare</i> 'to register' (cognate with registrarius), from registrum 'register', an alteration of Late Latin regesta "list, <a href = vnd.unilang:matters.html>matters</a> recorded", from the neuter plural of regestus, the past participle of regerere "to record, literally to carry back", itself from re- "back" + gerere "carry, bear"; the musical senses may well derive directly from register
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:registratie.html>registratie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:registratie.html>registraties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:registratie.html>registratietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A registration, the act of registering or being registered</li>
<li>An office in charge of registrations, especially when it also receives correlated payment of tax or other levies</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A registration, the act of selecting <a href = vnd.unilang:stops.html>stops</a> on an organ</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A specific setting thus achieved</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:reiger.html>reiger</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">heigero</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hraigrō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hraigrô</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. ***reisagent.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reisagent.html>reisagent</a> (48597)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reis.html>reis</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a></i>. Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">travel <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reisagent.html>reisagent</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reisagenten.html>reisagenten</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">reisagente</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A travel <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a>.</li></ol>

***reisgenoot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reisgenoot.html>reisgenoot</a> (36733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reis.html>reis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trip, journey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:genoot.html>genoot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fellow, companion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reisgenoot.html>reisgenoot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reisgenoten.html>reisgenoten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reisgenoot.html>reisgenootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">travel</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">companion</span>, who shares one's <span class="Latn" lang="en">company</span> on a <span class="Latn" lang="en">journey</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">reisen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*reison</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raisōną</i>.
